<userid>112119818775164229329</userid><name>Daniel Farias< /name>< date>
1561153526534< /date>
<rate>4<//rate>< review>
A really solid find in San Bernardino. The surrounding area isn't pretty but Nopal is pretty clean inside. The entire dining room could use a facelift but is otherwise in solid condition. Customer service is good, the lady who helped us out was very friendly. Prices are also comparable to most other Mexican establishments so that's good.

I've eaten a lot (and I mean a lot) of Mexican food but I've never seen a "Pamborazo" on the menu. 9 out of 10 times I'd go with tacos or enchiladas but considering I'd never had this before I decided to try it. This Pamborazo is basically a torta dipped in guajillo sauce and it comes with beans, chorizo, potatoes, lettuce, queso fresco and sour cream. Typically I would find something to pick on but in this case I wouldn't change a thing on this sandwich. My wife's huarache de asada was pretty good but the taco and complimentary chips and salsa were ok.

All in all this was a very good food stop. Customer service was good, food was good and an old dining room. If I'm ever in the area again I would definitely come back for more.< /review>

< Review>
Came here with my hubby and we were pleasantly surprised. Everything is freshly made from scratch. Authentic D.F. Style cuisine. I had the flautas de res, which were extra long on a big plate. My hubby had enchiladas rojas de pollo with beans and rice and they were very flavorful.  The cafe de olla is the best!!!  There is plenty of good parking. The inside is very nice and spacious. It has D.F. decor, photographs inside which is beautiful to reminisce of Mexico City, an awesome place to visit.  The service is stellar too. Very nice owner who came over to speak to us. We highly recommend this restaurant.< /Review>

Great food, great service. Fast service too considering I went during the dinner rush hour. It seems a bit pricey at first but the food is definitely worth it! <Review>This is my go-to place whenever we have people visiting Berkeley and want to get a large group together to eat. They always seem to have just enough space to fit our group, ranging anywhere from 4-10.

They have a great selection of burgers, all of them great. My personal favorites are Maui Waui, Baja, and Hickory.

The fries are delicious and come in huge portions. We usually get a full size serving of fries to split. The only fries I wouldn't recommend are the truffle fries. You can smell the truffle oil, but it doesn't really impact the taste, especially if you're going to be dipping them in ketchup.

Really generous portions. Expect to be stuffed by the time you're through with your burger and fries. If you get a shake in on top of that...well, good luck. I still feel full by the time I should be eating my next meal.<//Review>< date>
1582609227977</date>

< Review>
We got to the restaurant and it's pretty amazing! There is a great patio area and in the restaurant is cozy with wood furniture and a fireplace. There isn't a lot of street parking in this area but there is a Safeway right across the street.

The servers were really attentive to our needs and were really quick at taking our order. Food came out super quick. We ordered curly fries, the Big Barney, and the Voodoo Burger. The fries were on our table in less than 10 minutes and the our burgers were there in another 10 minutes. The fries were super fresh and hot. The ranch they have for it seems homemade and pairs well with the fries. Our burgers were hot and juicy. I would have liked my bun to be toasted and the pattie to be more heavily seasoned but it was still an excellent burger and nothing a salt shaker and pepper grinder could not fix (they were already there on the table along with ketchup, mustard, Dijon, and Tabasco).

Overall we had an excellent experience and I'm sure we'll be back soon.< /Review>

Now I know why everytime I go on about a giant hamburger someone asks me if I've been to Barney's ‚Äî these are burgers of epic proportions! I had the Morrocan burger, which was spicy, and topped with provolone and 1000 Island dressing (my prime condiment weakness). If I'm completely candid I miss some of the back in da day stuff,  before they consolidated the menu.  There used to be a greater variety of burger types (2 vegan options instead of one, more meat/fowl ones as well).

Everything was good.  If you want a burger with lots of choices for individualizing the condiments,  sauces,  embellishments - erm I mean toppings,  this is the place.  You'll leave super full!</Text>

<review>Quickie:
+ Lived in North Berkeley for 3 years during college and only one block away from the Gourmet Ghetto - so to say I frequented Barney's is an understatement.
+ Friggin' amazing burgers

---

Food:
What can I say? The burgers are delicious as are their fries (both steak cut and sweet potato). It's hard to narrow down but I think the French burger is my favorite (Crumbled Bleu cheese and bacon, yum). But in the number of times I've been there, I've probably tried over half the menu and my friends accounted for the rest. Always spectacular, very different combinations - just an all-around nice burger joint.

Overall:
They do take-out. as well, so if you have a midterm to cram for back at home, just call in and pick up in 15. All in all, Barney's is a great alternative to a greasy fast food burger - they do gourmet on a broke college kid's budget.< /review>< Gmap_id>
